+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+"""
+Test script to verify the fix for the keyspace ID issue.
+"""
+
+import subprocess
+import sys
+
+def run_check(description, command):
+    """Run a check command and print results"""
+    print(f"\n{description}...")
+    result = subprocess.run(command, shell=True, capture_output=True, text=True)
+    if result.returncode == 0 and result.stdout:
+        print(f"✓ {description} - PASSED")
+        if result.stdout.strip():
+            print(f"  Output: {result.stdout.strip()[:200]}")
+        return True
+    else:
+        print(f"✗ {description} - FAILED")
+        if result.stderr:
+            print(f"  Error: {result.stderr.strip()[:200]}")
+        return False
+
+def main():
+    print("="*80)
+    print("VERIFICATION OF KEYSPACE ID FIX")
+    print("="*80)
+
+    checks = []
+
+    # Check 1: groupCostController has keyspaceID field
+    print("\nCheck 1: Verify groupCostController struct has keyspaceID field")
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ["grep", "-A", "5", "type groupCostController struct", 
+         "/testbed/client/resource_group/controller/controller.go"],
+        capture_output=True, text=True
+    )
+    if "keyspaceID uint32" in result.stdout:
+        print("✓ groupCostController has keyspaceID field")
+        checks.append(True)
+    else:
+        print("✗ groupCostController does NOT have keyspaceID field")
+        checks.append(False)
+
+    # Check 2: newGroupCostController accepts keyspaceID parameter
+    print("\nCheck 2: Verify newGroupCostController accepts keyspaceID parameter")
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ["grep", "-A", "5", "func newGroupCostController", 
+         "/testbed/client/resource_group/controller/controller.go"],
+        capture_output=True, text=True
+    )
+    if "keyspaceID uint32" in result.stdout:
+        print("✓ newGroupCostController accepts keyspaceID parameter")
+        checks.append(True)
+    else:
+        print("✗ newGroupCostController does NOT accept keyspaceID parameter")
+        checks.append(False)
+
+    # Check 3: newGroupCostController sets keyspaceID in struct
+    print("\nCheck 3: Verify newGroupCostController sets keyspaceID in struct")
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ["grep", "-A", "15", "gc := &groupCostController{", 
+         "/testbed/client/resource_group/controller/controller.go"],
+        capture_output=True, text=True
+    )
+    if "keyspaceID: keyspaceID" in result.stdout:
+        print("✓ newGroupCostController sets keyspaceID in struct")
+        checks.append(True)
+    else:
+        print("✗ newGroupCostController does NOT set keyspaceID in struct")
+        checks.append(False)
+
+    # Check 4: collectRequestAndConsumption sets KeyspaceId in TokenBucketRequest
+    print("\nCheck 4: Verify collectRequestAndConsumption sets KeyspaceId in TokenBucketRequest")
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ["grep", "-A", "5", "func (gc \*groupCostController) collectRequestAndConsumption", 
+         "/testbed/client/resource_group/controller/controller.go"],
+        capture_output=True, text=True
+    )
+    if "KeyspaceId:" in result.stdout and "gc.keyspaceID" in result.stdout:
+        print("✓ collectRequestAndConsumption sets KeyspaceId in TokenBucketRequest")
+        checks.append(True)
+    else:
+        print("✗ collectRequestAndConsumption does NOT set KeyspaceId in TokenBucketRequest")
+        checks.append(False)
+
+    # Check 5: All calls to newGroupCostController pass keyspaceID
+    print("\nCheck 5: Verify all calls to newGroupCostController pass keyspaceID")
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ["grep", "newGroupCostController(", 
+         "/testbed/client/resource_group/controller/controller.go"],
+        capture_output=True, text=True
+    )
+    lines = result.stdout.strip().split('\n')
+    # Filter out the function definition
+    call_lines = [l for l in lines if 'func newGroupCostController' not in l]
+    all_have_keyspace = all('c.keyspaceID' in line for line in call_lines if line.strip())
+    if all_have_keyspace and len(call_lines) > 0:
+        print(f"✓ All {len(call_lines)} calls to newGroupCostController pass keyspaceID")
+        checks.append(True)
+    else:
+        print(f"✗ Not all calls to newGroupCostController pass keyspaceID")
+        print(f"  Found {len(call_lines)} calls")
+        for line in call_lines:
+            print(f"  - {line.strip()[:100]}")
+        checks.append(False)
+
+    # Check 6: Code compiles
+    print("\nCheck 6: Verify code compiles")
+    result = subprocess.run(
+        ["go", "build", "./..."],
+        cwd="/testbed/client/resource_group/controller",
+        capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=60
+    )
+    if result.returncode == 0:
+        print("✓ Code compiles successfully")
+        checks.append(True)
+    else:
+        print("✗ Code does NOT compile")
+        if result.stderr:
+            print(f"  Error: {result.stderr[:300]}")
+        checks.append(False)
+
+    # Summary
+    print("\n" + "="*80)
+    print("SUMMARY")
+    print("="*80)
+    passed = sum(checks)
+    total = len(checks)
+    print(f"Passed: {passed}/{total}")
+    
+    if all(checks):
+        print("\n✓ ALL CHECKS PASSED!")
+        print("\nThe fix successfully addresses the issue:")
+        print("  1. groupCostController now stores the keyspace ID")
+        print("  2. newGroupCostController accepts and sets the keyspace ID")
+        print("  3. collectRequestAndConsumption includes keyspace ID in TokenBucketRequest")
+        print("  4. All callers properly pass the keyspace ID")
+        print("  5. Code compiles without errors")
+        return 0
+    else:
+        print("\n✗ SOME CHECKS FAILED")
+        return 1
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    sys.exit(main())
